	Table 1:
	This table shows imported catch data, both catches were there are sample data
	(age or length data) and catches were there are no sample data.
	The data shown are ONLY CATCH DATA - NO AGE OR LENGTH DATA are shown.
	This means that for the sampled catches the sampled age or length data are cut of and not shown in table 1.
	Table 1 can be imported in a spreadsheet and used as a pivot table, to show data the way you want to see it.
	Remember Table 1 is tab delimited.

	Table 2:
	This table shows ALL catch data WITH AGE OR LENGTH DATA, both catches were there are sample data
	(age or length data) and catches were the age or length data have been estimated/hole filled.
